              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">

            <a aria-label="Opinion: City planners declare war on single-family home communities" class="article-card__link" href="/opinion/columnists/opinion-city-planners-declare-war-on-single-family-home-communities">
             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="Opinion: City planners declare war on single-family home communities">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               Opinion: City planners declare war on single-family home communities
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              March 22 is fast approaching, and your neighbourhood could change forever. A new law is on councils agenda. The City of Calgary has a plan to dispense with single-family neighbourhoods as we know them.
             </p>
            </a>
            <div class="article-card__meta-bottom">
             <span class="article-card__author">

             </span>

            <a aria-label="Chorney-Booth: Local vegetarian favourites come together under the new Nourish banner" class="article-card__link" href="/life/chorney-booth-local-vegetarian-favourites-come-together-under-the-new-nourish-banner">
             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="Chorney-Booth: Local vegetarian favourites come together under the new Nourish banner">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               Chorney-Booth: Local vegetarian favourites come together under the new Nourish banner
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              This last year has seen a lot of restaurant doors closing, but even as many businesses struggle, others have been able to embrace new opportunities. One sector that has been doing well (or more accurately, well-ish) over the last year has been Calgarys vegan and vegetarian eateries. Plant-based eaters yearn for pandemic-time comfort food as much as meat-lovers do and restaurants like VBurger, Nans Noodle House, and Vegan Street have been more than happy to serve up fresh and tasty meat-free takeout.
             </p>
            </a>

             </span>
